5< /rate>
< Review>
My wife got a Groupon deal for this place and it did not disappoint. This place is mainly a brewery/distillery it seems. I had and IPA and it was really tasty. They have an extensive menu of both beers/stouts as well as alcoholic pop they call Hard Frescoes. I did not sample the booze soda but one can just pop in and buy four packs of a large selection of the liquid menu items in tallboy cans. There is also food available with a largely south of the border feel. We shared a plate of tacos and some nachos which were super delicious. There was some sort of World/techno music playing which did not offend me. Big screen TVs to zone out on sports. The location is a bit out there, but it is easily accessible from the N-Judah. Because it is deep in the Sunset, street parking is probably pretty chill. I highly recommend this establishment and plan on going back for a night out very soon!<//Review>

< Review>
This is one of the best new places in the Outer Sunset! I am impressed with the food and though I am not much of a drinker, I know that I would have been impressed with the Artisan whiskeys and local Brews when I used to drink all the time. the atmosphere is super chill and I highly recommend Taco Thursday. I don't think there's Ada parking but since it's a fairly high traffic area cars come and go all the time, if you need a close parking space. it used to be the Lawton Tap House and now it is seven stills. Cheers, mate!<//Review>
